        if ("object" === typeof bbccookies && typeof bbccookies.readPolicy == 'function') {

        }
        if (noCookies && document.cookie.indexOf(cookiePrefix) !== -1) {
            //Find and remove cookies whose names begin with '_chartbeat'

            while (cookieLength--) {
